SELECT `a`.`Id`, `a`.`ArrivalTime`, `a`.`ChildId`, `a`.`CreatedAt`, `a`.`Date`, `a`.`DepartureTime`, `a`.`IsDeleted`, `a`.`IsEarlyLeave`, `a`.`IsLate`, `a`.`Notes`, `a`.`RecordedById`, `a`.`Status`, `a`.`UpdatedAt`, `t`.`Id`, `t`.`CreatedAt`, `t`.`DateOfBirth`, `t`.`FaceIdToken`, `t`.`FirstName`, `t`.`GroupId`, `t`.`IsDeleted`, `t`.`LastName`, `t`.`MonthlyFee`, `t`.`ParentEmail`, `t`.`ParentFullName`, `t`.`ParentPhone`, `t`.`RegistrationDate`, `t`.`ScheduleType`, `t`.`Status`, `t`.`UpdatedAt`, `t0`.`Id`, `t0`.`AgeCategory`, `t0`.`CreatedAt`, `t0`.`DivisionId`, `t0`.`IsDeleted`, `t0`.`Language`, `t0`.`MaxChildCount`, `t0`.`Name`, `t0`.`TeacherId`, `t0`.`UpdatedAt`
FROM `attendances` AS `a`
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT `c`.`Id`, `c`.`CreatedAt`, `c`.`DateOfBirth`, `c`.`FaceIdToken`, `c`.`FirstName`, `c`.`GroupId`, `c`.`IsDeleted`, `c`.`LastName`, `c`.`MonthlyFee`, `c`.`ParentEmail`, `c`.`ParentFullName`, `c`.`ParentPhone`, `c`.`RegistrationDate`, `c`.`ScheduleType`, `c`.`Status`, `c`.`UpdatedAt`
    FROM `children` AS `c`
    WHERE NOT (`c`.`IsDeleted`)
) AS `t` ON `a`.`ChildId` = `t`.`Id`
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT `g`.`Id`, `g`.`AgeCategory`, `g`.`CreatedAt`, `g`.`DivisionId`, `g`.`IsDeleted`, `g`.`Language`, `g`.`MaxChildCount`, `g`.`Name`, `g`.`TeacherId`, `g`.`UpdatedAt`
    FROM `groups` AS `g`
    WHERE NOT (`g`.`IsDeleted`)
) AS `t0` ON `t`.`GroupId` = `t0`.`Id`
WHERE NOT (`a`.`IsDeleted`) AND (`a`.`Id` = @__result_Id_0)
